               <h3>
                What is a Loan Rollover Offered to Customers?
               </h3>
               <p>
                There are many borrowers who, unfortunately, aren’t able to return the sums they obtained in time. What should they do with this debt? It’s not a problem for the majority of lenders because they often have the alternative to this situation. A payday loan store may propose an option called “rollover”. It’s a convenient method to delay your repayment period and save the money to cover the debt by the next deadline. You should notice that this option comes up with additional fees. For example, you borrowed 500 $ and had to pay 15 $ to every taken 100 $. In case you postponed the deadline and now you don’t know how to deal with this situation a lender will offer you to use the “rollover” feature with a fee. You can ask for two weeks more and return 75 $ and repay 500 $ by the end of this term. Everything will depend on the percentage rate of the sum you borrow. Pay attention that you will have to cover the added fee and return the total sum.

  <script>
   document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function(){
        var collapseBtn = document.querySelectorAll('.js-collapse-btn');
        for (var i = 0; i < collapseBtn.length; i++) {
            collapseBtn[i].addEventListener('click', collapseText);
        }
    });

    function collapseText(e) {
        var elem = e.target,
            value = elem.getAttribute("data-elem"),
            container = document.getElementById(value);
        elem.classList.toggle('is-open');
        container.classList.toggle('is-open');
    }
  </script>
